  <script type="application/ld+json">
   {"@context":"http://schema.org","headline":"The biggest stories of 2014","url":"http://mashable.com/2014/12/22/news-of-2014/","image":"http://rack.3.mshcdn.com/media/ZgkyMDE0LzEyLzIyLzBjL01hc2hhYmxlUGhvLmVmNzMxLmpwZwpwCXRodW1iCTEyMDB4NjI3IwplCWpwZw/a5f75d8c/ead/Mashable-Photos-Of-The-Year-2014-011.jpg","keywords":["video","news","space","israel","weather","russia","gaza","protests","hong-kong","uncategorized"],"@type":"Article","dateCreated":"2014-12-22T12:09:01Z","datePublished":"2014-12-22T12:09:01Z","articleSection":"world","creator":"Amanda Wills","author":"Amanda Wills","articleBody":"The biggest news of 2014\n\nThe events that defined our year\nJANUARY\n\nAmerica's first pot stores open in Colorado\nOn Jan. 1, Colorado became the first U.S. state to sell recreational marijuana, Washington state joined the party mid-year, and other states loosened their laws as well.\nAP Photo/Brennan Linsley\nPolar vortex\nSome areas dropped to their coldest temperatures in years as a polar vortex flooded the country from Canada, spreading into the Midwest and expanding to other states from coast to coast.\nCalifornia drought\nAfter record high temperatures and record low amounts of precipitation for much of the winter, California had a classic recipe for an intensifying drought that shows now sign of ending.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nFEBRUARY\n\nUkraine protests spur a revolution\nMonths of protests came to a tipping point when demonstrators clashed with police, leaving more than 70 people dead and leading to the ouster of president Viktor Yanukovych.Why it mattered: This led to the toppling of Ukraine's government and incited violence across the country. It was the beginning of Ukraine's ongoing battle with pro-Russian rebels.\nEPA/SERGEY DOLZHENKO\nWinter Olympics in Sochi\nFrom dancing bears to wipeouts in the snow, to political nightmares for Vladimir Putin, the Winter Olympics were filled with inspirational scenes, sports drama and a lot of weird moments.\nFacebook buys WhatsApp\nFacebook entered into an agreement to acquire WhatsApp, the popular messaging app, for $16 billion in cash and stock. The deal is by far Facebook's largest acquisition.\nMARCH\n\nMH370 vanishes\nMalaysia Airlines Flight 370 disappeared while en route from Kuala Lumpur to Beijing. A massive search operation was mounted across the Indian Ocean, but the Boeing 737 was never found. All 239 people on board are presumed dead. \nEPA/HOTLI SIMANJUNTAK!\nRussia annexes Crimea\nJust a few weeks after masked gunmen began popping up in Ukraine's Crimea region, Russian President Vladimir Putin annexed the peninsula and claimed it as part of Russia. Ukraine and Western leaders decried Putin's move, and piled on sanctions against the country as a result. \nEbola outbreak begins \nMore than 85 cases of Ebola were reported in Guinea in March, marking the beginning of an outbreak that quickly spread to Sierra Leone and Liberia. The surge would eventually become the largest Ebola epidemic in history. \nAPRIL\n\nHeartbleed attacks\nWebsites running SSL encryption \u2014 Gmail, Facebook, banks, just to name a few \u2014 were exposed to a major security bug called Heartbleed. The bug forced companies to update their servers with a security patch and users had to change their passwords. But even then it wasn't a guarantee that your information was safe. Why it mattered: Heartbleed is one of the biggest security threats the Internet has ever seen because it targeted encryption, which is the very thing that is supposed to keep us safe on the web. We will likely feel Heartbleed's effects for awhile. Two months after the bug, 300,000 web servers were still vulnerable.\nMashable composite\nNigeria schoolgirls kidnapped\nNearly 300 schoolgirls were kidnapped in April from the Government Secondary School in Chibok, Nigeria, by a radical Islamic group called Boko Haram. In early May, the hashtag #BringBackOurGirls began to spread on Twitter, raising the world's awareness of the mass abduction. Still, by year's end, a majority of the girls remained missing.\nSouth Korea ferry sinks\nMore than 300 passengers aboard a South Korean ferry, the MV Sewol, died on April 16 as a result of an \"unreasonably sudden turn.\" Many of the victims were high school students. The captain, along with 14 members of his crew, were charged with homicide, abandoning ship and negligence in the ferry's sinking. Its owner was found dead in July.\nMAY\n\nNew world leaders elected\nUkraine, India and Egypt were among the countries to hold high-stakes elections in May. On the brink of war, Ukraine elected chocolate billionaire and pro-European Union candidate Petro Poroshenko as president after the ouster of Viktor Yanukovych, who sided with Russia. India voted in Hindu nationalist Narendra Modi, a man who has his own checkered past, as prime minister. And nearly one year after protests led to a coup in which president Mohamed Morsi was overthrown, Abdel Fattah el-Sisi clinched the presidency with 96.91 percent of the vote.  \n\nApple buys Beats\nMay 28\nApple acquired Beats Electronics and Beats Music for $3 billion \u2014 by far the largest acquisition in its history. Beats cofounders Jimmy Iovine and Dr. Dre joined Apple. However the Beats brand will remain separate from Apple's. \n\u201cMusic is such an important part of all of our lives and holds a special place within our hearts at Apple.\u201d \u2014 Apple CEO Tim Cook\nJUNE\nISIS gains ground in Iraq\nAlthough the Islamic State (ISIS) began its rise in early 2014, the world took notice of the militant group when it embarked on a bloody campaign through Iraq in June, capturing city after city and forcing more than 1.7 million to flee. Why it mattered: ISIS has grown into one of the biggest radical threats in the world. The well-funded group has launched a massive online recruitment effort aimed at Westerners. The U.S. launched an airstrike campaign in both Iraq and Syria this year to help combat the group. \nJULY\n\nMH17 shot down in Ukraine\nTwo of the biggest stories of the year collided when a Malaysia Airlines flight was blown out of the sky in eastern Ukraine on July 17. All 298 people on board were killed. Ukraine and the West pointed the finger at Russia for supplying rebels with the weapons capable of downing a Boeing 777. The tragedy was the final push for a country already on the brink of war, and fighting between Ukrainian forces and pro-Russian rebels escalated in the region, prompting the U.S. and the European Union to impose more sanctions against Russia.\n\nWorld Cup\nGermany wins. Brazil suffers an epically embarrassing loss. USA's Tim Howard becomes a goalie god, and Uruguay's Luis Suarez bit a guy. The 2014 World Cup was one to remember.\nALS Ice Bucket Challenge\nIf you spent any time on the Internet this year, you've surely seen this one. The ALS Ice Bucket Challenge was an awareness campaign that spread through social media where users dared their friends to dump icy buckets of water over their heads. More than $100 million was raised as a result of the challenge, the majority of which will go towards finding a cure for the neurodegenerative disorder.\nAUGUST\nFerguson\nMichael Brown killed on August 9\nHours after a black, 18-year-old named Michael Brown was shot and killed by a white police officer, hundreds took to the streets of Ferguson, Missouri, to protest. But those demonstrations turned violent after police responded to looting with tear gas and rubber bullets. Why it mattered: Brown's death and the subsequent protests triggered a renewed debate about racism in America and the militarization of police. The Ferguson protests, which are still ongoing today, stretched nationwide, prompting the uprising of civil rights groups and even multiple statements from President Obama. \nRobin Williams dies at 63\nRobin Williams, the frenetic standup comedian and inimitable TV and film star whose richly dramatic side won him a supporting actor Oscar for Good Will Hunting, died at age 63 from an apparent suicide.\nCelebrity photo hack\nCelebrities including Jennifer Lawrence, Kate Upton, Victoria Justice and McKayla Maroney pursued legal action after a trove of their private nude photos \u2014 along with nude images of other celebrities \u2014 began spreading across the web in a massive hacking scandal that rocked Hollywood.\nSEPTEMBER\n\niPhone 6 and Apple Watch\nApple debuted a big iPhone 6 and an even bigger iPhone 6 Plus. But, wait, there's one more thing: The company also finally unveiled its long-awaited smartwatch.\n\nScotland votes No\nMillions voted in a referendum to decide whether Scotland should separate from the United Kingdom and become its own country. Although Scotland rejected independence and voted to stay with the UK, the referendum forever changed the political landscape.\nHong Kong protests\nTens of thousands of protesters blocked the streets of Hong Kong for 75 days to fight for democracy, shielding themselves from tear gas and pepper spray with surgical masks, goggles and umbrellas.\nOCTOBER\n\nEbola death toll tops 5,000\nAs Ebola swept West Africa, the death toll continued to rise with no end in sight due to porous borders and poor health care conditions. Meanwhile, the virus spread to the U.S. and Europe, inciting international panic about the virus, which currently has no cure. The United Nations also took responsibility for botching the initial response to the outbreak. Why it mattered: With the spread of Ebola and the spike in deaths, the world was forced to take notice at the situation in West Africa, and governments stepped in to help contain the virus in the region. \nKieran Kesner\nCanada parliament shooting\nA lone gunman with known mental health issues shot and killed a Canadian soldier on Ottawa's Parliament Hill, before entering Canada's parliament building and engaging in a shootout with security there. The 32-year-old Canadian man was shot dead by the Commons Sergeant at Arms, Kevin Vickers, in what Canadian police called a \"terrorist attack.\" The gunman's mother said he likely felt cornered by passport issues, \"so the only way out was death.\"\nBill Cosby rape scandal\nNearly two dozen women accused the comedian Bill Cosby of rape or sexual assaults that took place over a 40-year period. Cosby, 77, has denied all claims and has not been charged. As a result of the allegations, however, NBC scrapped plans for a Cosby project, Netflix put a special on hold and TV Land stopped airing reruns of \"The Cosby Show.\" Some of his performances were canceled and he lost a handful of honorary positions at various universities.\nNOVEMBER\nRosetta lands on a comet\nThe European Space Agency completed one of the biggest space feats in years when it landed a spacecraft on a comet speeding between Jupiter and Mars at nearly 40,000 mph. The Rosetta spacecraft dropped the refrigerator-sized Philae lander onto comet 67P/Churyumov-Gerasimenko, whose treacherous landscape is made up of plunging cliffs and rocky terrain. It was the first such landing of a space probe on a comet. The chance of success was just 70 percent. Why it mattered: Many scientists think comets were a crucial part of Earth's formation because they crashed into our planet during its formative years. Learning more about comets will ultimately reveal more about our own past.\nSony hack\nHackers broke into Sony's systems, leaking emails and other information to the public. The FBI later blamed the attack on North Korea, in retaliation for the comedy film \"The Interview.\"\nNo indictment in Ferguson\nDarren Wilson, the Ferguson police officer who fatally shot 18-year-old Michael Brown in August, was not indicted on any charges, a St. Louis County grand jury decided. After the announcement, protests turned violent, and many buildings were burned overnight. Demonstrations swept the U.S. for weeks.\nDECEMBER\n\nThe U.S. and Cuba mend their relationship\nThe U.S. and Cuba took a huge  step in mending diplomatic relations on Dec. 17 after Cuba released two Americans who had been imprisoned for years. \"We are choosing to cut loose the anchor of the past because it is entirely necessary to reach a better future \u2014 for our national interests, for the American people, and for the Cuban people,\u201d President Obama said in a historic speech. Raul Castro simultaneously addressed his nation, calling the move \"progress\" and saying that proves that it's \"possible to find a solution to many problems.\" \n\nEric Garner\nA black man accused of selling illegal cigarettes was killed by a white officer who put him in a chokehold in Staten Island, New York in July. When a grand jury failed to indict the officer, thousands took to the streets, chanting \"I can't breathe!\" and calling for the federal government to step in. Attorney General Eric Holder and President Obama both commented on the case, and said that the Justice Department had opened an investigation. It is still underway.\nSydney hostage crisis\nA lone gunman took 17 hostages captive in a Sydney chocolate shop in December, forcing them to display a black flag with white Arabic letters, and requested a conversation with Australia's prime minister, suggesting to the world's media that the action was a terror attack. Sixteen hours later, the Australian police stormed the cafe and shot dead the gunman. Two hostages were killed in the firefight and four others were injured. Australian officials said the siege was an isolated incident, and not a coordinated terror incident.\n                                            Share                Tweet                                                                                          \n\n\nEditor:\nAmanda Wills\n\n\nVideo:\nChris Grasinger &amp; Heather Martino\n\n\nAdditional reporting:\nBrian Ries\n\n","mainEntityOfPage":"True","metadata":{"page":1,"omnitureData":{"channel":"world","content_type":"article","v_buy":null,"v_buy_i":null,"h_pub":4853.5,"h_buy":null,"h_pub_buy":null,"v_cur":1.9,"v_max":2.1,"v_cur_i":1,"v_max_i":2,"events":"event51,event61","top_channel":"world","content_source_type":"Internal","content_source_name":"Internal","author_name":"Amanda Wills","age":"202","pub_day":22,"pub_month":12,"pub_year":2014,"pub_date":"12/22/2014","sourced_from":"Internal","isPostView":true,"post_lead_type":"Longform","topics":"Climate,eric garner,Protests in Ferguson, Missouri ,Israel and Gaza,Mashable Must Reads,Hong Kong,Isis,Islamic State,Israel,news,polar vortex,protests,russia,Space,Ukraine ,Uncategorized,U.S.,World,Video","campaign":null,"display_mode":null,"viral_video_type":null,"b_flag":true},"postId":3105477}}

         <p class="title">

         <h1>
          America's first pot stores open in Colorado
         </h1>
         <p class="caption">
          On Jan. 1, Colorado became the first U.S. state to sell recreational marijuana, Washington state joined the party mid-year, and other states loosened their laws as well.
         </p>

          Polar vortex
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-two">
          Some areas dropped to their coldest temperatures in years as a polar vortex flooded the country from Canada, spreading into the Midwest and expanding to other states from coast to coast.

         <p class="title">
         </p>
         <h1>
          Ukraine protests spur a revolution
         </h1>
         <p class="caption">
          Months of protests came to a tipping point when demonstrators clashed with police, leaving more than 70 people dead and leading to the ouster of president Viktor Yanukovych.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <strong>
           Why it mattered:
          </strong>
          This led to the toppling of Ukraine's government and incited violence across the country. It was the beginning of Ukraine's ongoing battle with pro-Russian rebels.
         </p>
         <p class="credit">
          EPA/SERGEY DOLZHENKO
         </p>

         <h2 class="name">

         <h1>
          MH370 vanishes
         </h1>
         <p class="caption">
          Malaysia Airlines Flight 370 disappeared while en route from Kuala Lumpur to Beijing. A massive search operation was mounted across the Indian Ocean, but the Boeing 737 was never found. All 239 people on board are presumed dead.
         </p>
         <p class="credit">
          EPA/HOTLI SIMANJUNTAK!
         </p>

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text bio-text" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <h2 class="name">
          Russia annexes Crimea
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-two">
          Just a few weeks after masked gunmen began popping up in Ukraine's Crimea region, Russian President Vladimir Putin
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2014/03/16/crimea-votes-secede-ukraine/">
           annexed the peninsula
          </a>
          and claimed it as part of Russia. Ukraine and Western leaders decried Putin's move, and piled on sanctions against the country as a result.
         </p>
        </div>

         <h2 class="name">
          Ebola outbreak begins
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-two">
          More than 85 cases of Ebola were reported in Guinea in March, marking the beginning of an outbreak that quickly spread to Sierra Leone and Liberia. The surge would eventually become the largest Ebola epidemic in history.

       <div class="long-card parsec-card image-card infographic-card v0" data-breakpoint="[&quot;x\x9CM\x90\xC1n\x830\f\x86_\xC5\xE2\xD4Nm\x02\t\xA5\xC0y\xD2\xAE\xD3v\xAD\x84\x02\xB8m\xB4\x10\xBA$\xC0\xAAi\xEF&gt;\xA7\xEB\xA6\xE5d\xC7\xF6\xEF\xCF\xFFgrT\x9D6:\\\x93:yQ\xDAxX=\xBB\xB1\x9F\xBA\xA0G\xBBN6\xC9\x8C\xCESH\xE5\x8C\xA5\x94\x9FG\x1F(\x91\xA2\xAA2\xB1]\xB0\xDD\xB1A\xF9\xB3j\r\xB2n\x1C\xA8\xC3\xE0\x8C&amp;\xA9\x8BM\xE2\xCF\xA3\v\xCD\x80\xDE\xAB\x13\xD2\xD0\xC1&gt;\xC4\a\x8F\xD8N\xA7\x13:p\xF8&gt;\xA1\x0F\xD8o\xA0\x9D\x02,\xCA\x83\x1D\x03\xA8\x99H\xA2\&quot;\xAC\xD0\xFA\xC9!\xB8\xA9\xBDn\xFB8\x06\xDA\x83\xD1q\x06\xB4\x85'\x1C\x8E\xDA \xD7\xD6\ae\f}\x92\xC4\t\x87u\r\xAFA\xB9\x00\x1E\x1D]\x00\x8B\x0Eg\xD8\xFE(\xC4\xC5a\x04\xB4\xB7\r7\xA2\x83%\xEE;L\xA3{B-\x8B\xFC\x98\xE3\xBE\x10\x12\xD3TJ\xD9\xE5U/v\xBD\xC0L\xC9\xB4J[\xEA\x8F\x8B\xA9\x93\xCF\xCA\xF1eY\xF8\x1C\xAD\xF1\xFC\xBF\e\x7FI3\vN\x91\xC3\x9E\xB7\x93\xED\x898^\xC4\x05KY\xCA\x89\xD7sE\x8E\xCF\xE8\xA7\xCB\x85&lt;\xDBJ&amp;XVr\xA3\xDB{\xA1\xB9Wx7:l\xF0#\xF07t\x16\r\xFF=\x89\xB9\xC8d\xB4\xC5\x9B\xF5A\x93\xEDA\r\x97\xA4\xCErY\xEC\x85,E\xC9v\xFB\xA2*\x8B\xF2\xEB\eu\x89\xA7\x04&quot;]" data-chapter="" data-chapter-fragment="" data-chapter-image="" data-extended-options="{}" data-height-style="" data-style="{}" data-title="Card" data-type="LongCard" id="" style="">
        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-image infographic-block image-wrap" data-click-through-url="" data-native-height="" data-native-width="" data-type="ImageBlock" data-url="http://rack.3.mshcdn.com/media/ZgkyMDE0LzA4LzI1LzE3L0hlYXJ0YmxlZWRSLmVkNDc3LmpwZwpwCXRodW1iCTk1MHg1MzQjCmUJanBn/3e5b392b/662/Heartbleed-Refresh.jpg">
         <img onload="if(App.Parsec.container){App.Parsec.container.resize();}" src="http://rack.3.mshcdn.com/media/ZgkyMDE0LzA4LzI1LzE3L0hlYXJ0YmxlZWRSLmVkNDc3LmpwZwpwCXRodW1iCTk1MHg1MzQjCmUJanBn/3e5b392b/662/Heartbleed-Refresh.jpg"/>
        </div>
        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text text-wrap infographic-block" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <p class="title">
         </p>
         <h1>
          Heartbleed attacks
         </h1>
         <p class="caption">
          Websites running SSL encryption  Gmail, Facebook, banks, just to name a few  were exposed to a major security bug called Heartbleed. The bug forced companies to update their servers with a security patch and users had to change their passwords. But even then it wasn't a guarantee that your information was safe.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <strong>
           Why it mattered:
          </strong>
          Heartbleed is one of the biggest security threats the Internet has ever seen because it targeted encryption, which is the very thing that is supposed to keep us safe on the web. We will likely feel Heartbleed's effects for awhile. Two months after the bug, 300,000 web servers were still vulnerable.
         </p>
         <p class="credit">
          Mashable composite
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

         <img onload="if(App.Parsec.container){App.Parsec.container.resize();}" src="http://1.mshcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/Nigeria-Missing-Girls.jpg"/>

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text bio-text" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <h2 class="name">
          Nigeria schoolgirls kidnapped
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-two">
          Nearly 300 schoolgirls were kidnapped in April from the Government Secondary School in Chibok, Nigeria, by a radical Islamic group called Boko Haram. In early May, the hashtag #BringBackOurGirls began to spread on Twitter, raising the world's awareness of the mass abduction. Still, by year's end, a majority of the girls remained missing.
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="long-card parsec-card bio-card v0 bio-image-center" data-breakpoint="[&quot;x\x9CM\x90\xC1n\x830\f\x86_\xC5\xE2\xD4N%\x81\xA4P\xDA\xF3\xA4]\xA7\xEDZ\t\x05pi\xB4\x10\xBA$\xC0\xAAi\xEF&gt;\xA7\xEB\xA6\xE5d\xC7\xF6\xEF\xCF\xFFgrR\xAD6:\\\x93C\xF2\xA2\xB4\xF1\xB0zvc7\xB5A\x8Fv\x9Dl\x92\x19\x9D\xA7\x90\xCA9\xCB(?\x8F&gt;P\&quot;\xC5~\x9F\x8Bt\xC1\xA6`\x83\xF2g\xD5\x18d\xED8P\x87\xC1\x19Mr(7\x89?\x8F.\xD4\x03z\xAFz\xA4\xA1\xA3}\x88\x0F\x1E\xB1\x99\xFA\x1E\x1D8|\x9F\xD0\a\xEC6\xD0L\x01\x16\xE5\xC1\x8E\x01\xD4L$Q\x11Vh\xFD\xE4\x10\xDC\xD4\\\xD3.\x8E\x81\xF6`t\x9C\x01m\xE1\t\x87\x936\xC8\xB5\xF5A\x19C\x9F$\xD1\xE3\xB0&gt;\xC0kP.\x80GG\x17\xC0\xA2\xC3\x19\xD2\x1F\x85\xB88\x8C\x80\xF6\xB6\xE1Ft\xB4\xC4}\x87\xA9uG\xA8U\xB9=mqW\n\x89Y&amp;\xA5l\xB7\xFBN\x14\x9D\xC0\\\xC9l\x9F5\xD4\x1F\x17S'\x9F\x95\xE3\xCB\xB2\xF09Z\xE3\xF9\x7F7\xFE\x92z\x16\x9C\&quot;\x87\x1Do&amp;\xDB\x11q\xBC\x88\v\x96\xB1\x8C\x13\xAF\xE7\x8A\x1C\x9F\xD1O\x97\vy\x96J&amp;X^q\xA3\x9B{\xA1\xBEWx;:\xAC\xF1#\xF07t\x16\r\xFF=\x89\xB9\xC8d\xB4\xC5\x9B\xF5A\x93\xEDA\r\x97\xE4\x90oe\xB9\x13\xB2\x12\x15+\xAA\&quot;\x13\xF9\xD77\xCE|\xA6\xB8&quot;]" data-chapter="" data-chapter-fragment="" data-chapter-image="" data-extended-options="{}" data-height-style="" data-style="{}" data-title="Card" data-type="LongCard" id="" style="">

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text bio-text" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <h2 class="name">
          South Korea ferry sinks
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-two">
          More than 300 passengers aboard a South Korean ferry, the MV Sewol, died on April 16 as a result of an "unreasonably sudden turn." Many of the victims were high school students. The captain, along with 14 members of his crew, were charged with homicide, abandoning ship and negligence in the ferry's sinking. Its owner was found dead in July.
         </p>
        </div>

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text text-wrap" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <p class="title">
         </p>
         <h1>
          New world leaders elected
         </h1>
         <p class="caption">
          Ukraine, India and Egypt were among the countries to hold high-stakes elections in May. On the brink of war, Ukraine elected
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2014/05/25/ukraine-president-petro-poroshenko/" style="color:#b1e3fa;">
           chocolate billionaire
          </a>
          and pro-European Union candidate Petro Poroshenko as president after the ouster of Viktor Yanukovych, who sided with Russia. India voted in Hindu nationalist Narendra Modi, a man
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2014/05/16/narendra-modi-india-elections/" style="color:#b1e3fa;">
           who has his own checkered past
          </a>
          , as prime minister. And nearly one year after protests led to a coup in which president Mohamed Morsi was overthrown, Abdel Fattah el-Sisi clinched the presidency with 96.91 percent of the vote.
         </p>
         <p class="credit">
         </p>

         <h2 class="name">
          Apple buys Beats
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-one">
          May 28
         </p>
         <p class="detail-two">
          Apple acquired Beats Electronics and Beats Music for $3 billion  by far the largest acquisition in its history. Beats cofounders Jimmy Iovine and Dr. Dre joined Apple. However the Beats brand will remain separate from Apple's.
         </p>

         </p>

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text bio-text" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <h2 class="name">
          ISIS gains ground in Iraq
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-two">
          Although the Islamic State (ISIS) began its rise in early 2014, the world took notice of the militant group when it embarked on a bloody campaign through Iraq in June, capturing city after city and forcing more than
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2014/10/28/on-the-run-from-isis/">
           1.7 million to flee
          </a>
          .
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <strong>
           Why it mattered:
          </strong>
          ISIS has grown into one of the biggest radical threats in the world. The well-funded group has launched a massive online recruitment effort aimed at Westerners. The U.S. launched an airstrike campaign in both Iraq and Syria this year to help combat the group.
         </p>
        </div>

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-image mobile-static-fallback" data-click-through-url="" data-native-height="" data-native-width="" data-type="ImageBlock" data-url="http://1.mshcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/MH17-Ukraine-Plane-Crash.jpg">

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text text-wrap" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <p class="title">
         </p>
         <h1>
          MH17 shot down in Ukraine
         </h1>
         <p class="caption">
          Two of the biggest stories of the year collided when a Malaysia Airlines flight
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2014/07/17/malaysia-airlines-ukraine/" style="color:#b1e3fa;">
           was blown out of the sky
          </a>
          in eastern Ukraine on July 17. All 298 people on board were killed. Ukraine and the West
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2014/07/17/malaysia-airlines-ukraine-russia-rebel/" style="color:#b1e3fa;">
           pointed the finger at Russia
          </a>
          for supplying rebels with
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2014/07/17/malaysia-mh17-ukraine-what-shot-down/" style="color:#b1e3fa;">
           the weapons capable of downing a Boeing 777
          </a>
          . The tragedy was the final push for a country already on the brink of war, and fighting between Ukrainian forces and pro-Russian rebels escalated in the region, prompting the U.S. and the European Union to impose more sanctions against Russia.
         </p>
         <p class="credit">
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text bio-text" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <h2 class="name">
          ALS Ice Bucket Challenge
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-two">
          If you spent any time on the Internet this year, you've surely seen this one. The ALS Ice Bucket Challenge was an awareness campaign that spread through social media where users dared their friends to dump icy buckets of water over their heads. More than $100 million was raised as a result of the challenge, the majority of which will go towards finding a cure for the neurodegenerative disorder.
         </p>

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text bio-text" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <h2 class="name">
          Ferguson
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-one">
          Michael Brown killed on August 9
         </p>
         <p class="detail-two">
          Hours after a black, 18-year-old named Michael Brown was shot and killed by a white police officer, hundreds took to the streets of Ferguson, Missouri, to protest. But those demonstrations
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2014/08/19/ferguson-missouri-protesters/">
           turned violent
          </a>
          after police responded to looting with tear gas and rubber bullets.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <strong>
           Why it mattered:
          </strong>
          Brown's death and the subsequent protests
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2014/08/24/people-of-ferguson-missouri/">
           triggered a renewed debate about racism in America
          </a>
          and the militarization of police. The Ferguson protests,
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2014/10/10/ferguson-raw-city/">
           which are still ongoing today
          </a>
          , stretched nationwide, prompting the uprising of civil rights groups and even multiple statements from President Obama.
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

         </h2>
         <p class="detail-two">
          Millions voted in a referendum to decide whether Scotland should separate from the United Kingdom and become its own country. Although

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text bio-text" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <h2 class="name">
          Hong Kong protests
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-two">
          Tens of thousands of protesters blocked the streets of Hong Kong for 75 days to fight for democracy, shielding themselves from tear gas and pepper spray with surgical masks, goggles and umbrellas.
         </p>
        </div>

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-image mobile-static-fallback" data-click-through-url="" data-native-height="" data-native-width="" data-type="ImageBlock" data-url="http://1.mshcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/Kieran-Kesner-Liberia-11.jpg">

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text text-wrap" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <p class="title">
         </p>
         <h1>
          Ebola death toll tops 5,000
         </h1>
         <p class="caption">
          As Ebola swept West Africa, the death toll continued to rise with no end in sight due to porous borders and poor health care conditions. Meanwhile, the virus spread to the U.S. and Europe, inciting international panic about the virus, which currently has no cure. The United Nations also took responsibility for
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2014/10/17/un-who-ebola-outbreak-botched/" style="color:#b1e3fa;">
           botching the initial response
          </a>
          to the outbreak.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <strong>
           Why it mattered:
          </strong>
          With the spread of Ebola and the
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2014/10/22/ebola-numbers-death-toll-cases/" style="color:#b1e3fa;">
           spike in deaths
          </a>
          , the world was forced to take notice at the situation in West Africa, and governments stepped in to help contain the virus in the region.
         </p>
         <p class="credit">
          Kieran Kesner
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text bio-text" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <h2 class="name">
          Canada parliament shooting
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-two">
          A lone gunman with known mental health issues shot and killed a Canadian soldier on Ottawa's Parliament Hill, before entering Canada's parliament building and engaging in a shootout with security there. The 32-year-old Canadian man was shot dead by the Commons Sergeant at Arms, Kevin Vickers, in what Canadian police called a "terrorist attack." The gunman's mother said he likely felt cornered by passport issues, "so the only way out was death."
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text bio-text" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <h2 class="name">
          Bill Cosby rape scandal
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-two">
          Nearly two dozen women accused the comedian Bill Cosby of rape or sexual assaults that took place over a 40-year period. Cosby, 77, has denied all claims and has not been charged. As a result of the allegations, however, NBC scrapped plans for a Cosby project, Netflix put a special on hold and TV Land stopped airing reruns of "The Cosby Show." Some of his performances were canceled and he lost a handful of honorary positions at various universities.
         </p>
        </div>

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-image bio-image" data-click-through-url="" data-native-height="" data-native-width="" data-type="ImageBlock" data-url="http://1.mshcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Comet-5.jpg">
         <img onload="if(App.Parsec.container){App.Parsec.container.resize();}" src="http://1.mshcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Comet-5.jpg"/>

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text bio-text" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <h2 class="name">
          Rosetta lands on a comet
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-two">
          The European Space Agency completed one of the biggest space feats in years when it
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2014/11/11/rosetta-philae-comet-landing/">
           landed a spacecraft on a comet
          </a>
          speeding between Jupiter and Mars at nearly 40,000 mph. The Rosetta spacecraft dropped the refrigerator-sized Philae lander onto comet 67P/Churyumov-Gerasimenko, whose treacherous landscape is made up of plunging cliffs and rocky terrain. It was the first such landing of a space probe on a comet. The chance of success was just 70 percent.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <strong>
           Why it mattered:
          </strong>
          Many scientists think comets were a crucial part of Earth's formation because they crashed into our planet during its formative years. Learning more about comets will ultimately reveal more about our own past.
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>

         <h2 class="name">
          Sony hack
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-two">
          Hackers broke into Sony's systems, leaking emails and other information to the public. The FBI later blamed the attack on North Korea, in retaliation for the comedy film "The Interview."
         </p>

         <h2 class="name">
          No indictment in Ferguson
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-two">
          Darren Wilson, the Ferguson police officer who fatally shot 18-year-old Michael Brown in August, was not indicted on any charges, a St. Louis County grand jury decided. After the announcement, protests turned violent, and many buildings were burned overnight. Demonstrations swept the U.S. for weeks.

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-image mobile-static-fallback" data-click-through-url="" data-native-height="" data-native-width="" data-type="ImageBlock" data-url="http://1.mshcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/Cuba1.jpg">

        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text text-wrap" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <p class="title">
         </p>
         <h1>
          The U.S. and Cuba mend their relationship
         </h1>
         <p class="caption">
          The U.S. and Cuba took a huge  step in
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2014/12/17/live-cuba-us-deal/" style="color:#b1e3fa;">
           mending diplomatic relations
          </a>
          on Dec. 17 after Cuba
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2014/12/17/cuba-alan-gross-released/" style="color:#b1e3fa;">
           released two Americans
          </a>
          who had been imprisoned for years. "We are choosing to cut loose the anchor of the past because it is entirely necessary to reach a better future  for our national interests, for the American people, and for the Cuban people, President Obama said in a
          <a href="http://mashable.com/2014/12/17/us-cuba-relationship-reboot/" style="color:#b1e3fa;">
           historic speech
          </a>
          . Raul Castro simultaneously addressed his nation, calling the move "progress" and saying that proves that it's "possible to find a solution to many problems."
         </p>
         <p class="credit">
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="long-card parsec-card bio-card v0 bio-image-center" data-breakpoint="[&quot;x\x9CM\x90MO\xC30\f\x86\xFF\x8A\xD5\xD3\x86\xB6\xA4M\xB6\xEE\xE3\x8C\xC4\x15\xC1uR\x95\xB6^\e\x91&amp;#I[&amp;\xC4\x7F\xC7\x19\x03\x91\x93\x1D\xDB\xAF\x1F\xBF\x9F\xD9Y5\xDA\xE8x\xCD\x8E\xD9\x8B\xD2&amp;\xC0\xE2\xD9\xBBvl\xA2vv\x99\xAD\xB2\t}\xA0\x90\xCA\x05\xCB)\xEF]\x88\x94Hq8\x14b=c\xBDe\x83\n\xBD\xAA\r\xB2\xC6\r\xD4apB\x93\x1D\xCBU\x16z\xE7c5`\b\xAAC\x1A:\xD9\x87\xF4\xE0\x11\xEB\xB1\xEB\xD0\x83\xC7\xF7\x11C\xC4v\x05\xF5\x18aV\x01\xAC\x8B\xA0&amp;\&quot;I\x8A\xB0@\eF\x8F\xE0\xC7\xFA\xBAn\xD3\x18\xE8\x00F\xA7\x19\xD0\x16\x9Ep8k\x83\\\xDB\x10\x951\xF4I\x12\x1D\x0E\xCB#\xBCF\xE5#\x04\xF4t\x01\xCC:\xF6\xB0\xFEQH\x8B\xA3\x03\xB4\xB7\r7\xA2\x93%\xEE;L\xA5[B\xDD\x97\x9B\xF3\x06w\xA5\x90\x98\xE7R\xCAfsh\xC5\xB6\x15X(\x99\x1F\xF2\x9A\xFA\xD3b\xEA\xE4\x93\xF2|\x9Eg&gt;%k\x02\xFF\xEF\xC6_RM\x82S\xE4\xB1\xE5\xF5h[\&quot;N\x17q\xC1r\x96s\xE2\r\\\x91\xE3\x13\x86\xF1r!\xCF\xD6\x92\tV\xEC\xB9\xD1\xF5\xBDP\xDD+\xBCq\x1E+\xFC\x88\xFC\r\xBDE\xC3\x7FOb&gt;1\x19m\xF1f}\xD4d{T\xC3%;\x16\eY\xEE\x84\xDC\x8B=\xDB\x89m\x99\x8B\xE2\xEB\eu'\xA6\xEA&quot;]" data-chapter="" data-chapter-fragment="" data-chapter-image="" data-extended-options="{}" data-height-style="" data-style="{}" data-title="Card" data-type="LongCard" id="" style="">
        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-image bio-image" data-click-through-url="" data-native-height="" data-native-width="" data-type="ImageBlock" data-url="http://1.mshcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/Screen-Shot-2014-12-21-at-10.47.53-AM.png">
         <img onload="if(App.Parsec.container){App.Parsec.container.resize();}" src="http://1.mshcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/Screen-Shot-2014-12-21-at-10.47.53-AM.png"/>
        </div>
        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text bio-text" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <h2 class="name">
          Eric Garner
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-two">
          A black man accused of selling illegal cigarettes was killed by a white officer who put him in a chokehold in Staten Island, New York in July. When a grand jury failed to indict the officer, thousands took to the streets, chanting "I can't breathe!" and calling for the federal government to step in. Attorney General Eric Holder and President Obama both commented on the case, and said that the Justice Department had opened an investigation. It is still underway.
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="long-card parsec-card bio-card v0 bio-image-center" data-breakpoint="[&quot;x\x9CM\x90\xC1n\x830\f\x86_\xC5\xE2\xD4Nm\x02\t\xA5\xC0y\xD2\xAE\xD3v\xAD\x84\x02\xB8m\xB4\x10\xBA$\xC0\xAAi\xEF&gt;\xA7\xEB\xA6\xE5d\xC7\xF6\xEF\xCF\xFFgrT\x9D6:\\\x93:yQ\xDAxX=\xBB\xB1\x9F\xBA\xA0G\xBBN6\xC9\x8C\xCESH\xE5\x8C\xA5\x94\x9FG\x1F(\x91\xA2\xAA2\xB1]\xB0\xDD\xB1A\xF9\xB3j\r\xB2n\x1C\xA8\xC3\xE0\x8C&amp;\xA9\x8BM\xE2\xCF\xA3\v\xCD\x80\xDE\xAB\x13\xD2\xD0\xC1&gt;\xC4\a\x8F\xD8N\xA7\x13:p\xF8&gt;\xA1\x0F\xD8o\xA0\x9D\x02,\xCA\x83\x1D\x03\xA8\x99H\xA2\&quot;\xAC\xD0\xFA\xC9!\xB8\xA9\xBDn\xFB8\x06\xDA\x83\xD1q\x06\xB4\x85'\x1C\x8E\xDA \xD7\xD6\ae\f}\x92\xC4\t\x87u\r\xAFA\xB9\x00\x1E\x1D]\x00\x8B\x0Eg\xD8\xFE(\xC4\xC5a\x04\xB4\xB7\r7\xA2\x83%\xEE;L\xA3{B-\x8B\xFC\x98\xE3\xBE\x10\x12\xD3TJ\xD9\xE5U/v\xBD\xC0L\xC9\xB4J[\xEA\x8F\x8B\xA9\x93\xCF\xCA\xF1eY\xF8\x1C\xAD\xF1\xFC\xBF\e\x7FI3\vN\x91\xC3\x9E\xB7\x93\xED\x898^\xC4\x05KY\xCA\x89\xD7sE\x8E\xCF\xE8\xA7\xCB\x85&lt;\xDBJ&amp;XVr\xA3\xDB{\xA1\xB9Wx7:l\xF0#\xF07t\x16\r\xFF=\x89\xB9\xC8d\xB4\xC5\x9B\xF5A\x93\xEDA\r\x97\xA4\xCErY\xEC\x85,E\xC9\xF6\xA2\xCA\x8B\xFC\xEB\e\xCE\x9C\xA6\xC3&quot;]" data-chapter="" data-chapter-fragment="" data-chapter-image="" data-extended-options="{}" data-height-style="" data-style="{}" data-title="Card" data-type="LongCard" id="" style="">
        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-image bio-image" data-click-through-url="" data-native-height="" data-native-width="" data-type="ImageBlock" data-url="http://1.mshcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/Screen-Shot-2014-12-21-at-10.49.56-AM.png">
         <img onload="if(App.Parsec.container){App.Parsec.container.resize();}" src="http://1.mshcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/Screen-Shot-2014-12-21-at-10.49.56-AM.png"/>
        </div>
        <div class="parsec-block parsec-block-text bio-text" data-style="{}" data-type="TextBlock" style="">
         <h2 class="name">
          Sydney hostage crisis
         </h2>
         <p class="detail-two">
          A lone gunman took 17 hostages captive in a Sydney chocolate shop in December, forcing them to display a black flag with white Arabic letters, and requested a conversation with Australia's prime minister, suggesting to the world's media that the action was a terror attack. Sixteen hours later, the Australian police stormed the cafe and shot dead the gunman. Two hostages were killed in the firefight and four others were injured. Australian officials said the siege was an isolated incident, and not a coordinated terror incident.
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
